				<article id="post-4784" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-4784 page type-page status-publish hentry grow-content-main">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4784_13abe8-f1 alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-layout-overlay kt-row-overlay-normal"></div><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4784_01ec90-45 kb-section-has-overlay kb-section-dir-vertical inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading4784_3afdb6-15 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_3afdb6-15"><strong>Musafir in Transit </strong></h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4784_15c96d-24 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_15c96d-24"><em>Part travelogue, part field notes, part trial and error.</em></p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4784_169cb4-8b alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4784_325425-c9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4784_7a3467-5d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-5-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_7a3467-5d">Behind the chaos</h2>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4784_51b029-96 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-5-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_51b029-96"> </h2>



<p><strong>Hi, I’m Hira</strong> &#8211; a Pakistani traveler with a stubborn passport, a soft spot for mountains, and a long track record of questionable decisions that somehow make great stories.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4784_db4fa8-3b_0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_db4fa8-3b_0">Over the past 7+ years, I’ve slow-traveled through 20+ countries across four continents. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4784_bd079d-28_2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_bd079d-28_2">I write about navigating the world as a woman of colour, the logistics of slow travel in misrepresented places, and the joy of going offbeat (sometimes accidentally). Expect destination guides, cultural commentary, and stories I probably shouldn’t tell on the internet.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4784_a0cfde-dd wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4784_a0cfde-dd">You can <a href="/about/"><strong>read the full story</strong></a>, or <a href="/contact/"><strong>get in touch</strong></a> &#8211; I genuinely love hearing from people who read this blog!</p>
